<Time>1607407719446</Time><Rating>1</Rating><Review>15 years ago I found this Vet when my cat was very sick.  Dr Salwan was amazing, kind and helped me through a cancer diagnosis and treatment.  Never had any issues with the staff, etc.  Years later, my other cat came down with the same cancer and Dr Salwan was again, very helpful and compassionate.

Fast forward to now and the story is VASTLY different.  I called last Sunday to get help for my 1.5yr cat who hadn't used the litter box is a few days and was vomiting liquid (he is known to try to eat anything he can find, just like a puppy).  They could not see him.  Not only that but the girl on the other end of the line was rude and dismissive.  What a horrible way to treat someone who has a sick animal.  I ended up taking kitty to Beacon for emergency service.  They were compassionate, responsive and helpful.  Bloodwork, x-rays, fluids......unfortunately no diagnosis was found.

Follow up today with his regular vet and we saw Dr Salwan.  I was hopeful for the same good service I'd once had.  I left kitty for x-rays and expected a call back to discuss next step.  3 hrs later I called to check, the answer was simply "you can come pick him up now".  Wait, what?  What's wrong with him?  How are we going to fix it?  Nobody has contacted me.  I am then told oh sorry, x-ray results take 1-2 days, doctor will talk to you then.  I'm sorry but the cat is not eating, is dehydrated and has not had a bowel movement in a week.  I am absolutely disgusted with this service.  This is a life we are talking about, a member of my family.  I have now spent $1600 and my cat is still very sick with no path forward.  This is unacceptable.  What has happened to this place?

Additionally, I neglected to comment on the fact that I had a similar incident in August with my 9yo cat.  Took days to get results from his x-rays.  Many phone calls, thankfully, his was a minor issue and was resolved easily.......luckily.

Dr Salwan is a good Vet, WHEN he is onsite.  Seems he doesn't work there much anymore and the staff is overworked and frustrated.  This may be an OK place if you need simple things like vaccinations or a simply check-up.  But for Gods sake, don't bring your animal here if it is ill, who knows how long it will take to get them checked IF they can even see you when you need to be seen.

<name>Jeff Bond<//name>< review>
GREAT ... service, doctors, and prices !

The doctors know what they're doing, if you provide good details of the conditions your pet is experiencing, they're good at getting to the root cause, and properly addressing the issue.

If you just show up, they want to do a round of diagnostics as a baseline to work with, which makes complete sense.

i had a dog who got a a large splinter embedded under their skin that the doctor at first thought was a possible tumor, so he wanted to do more investigation.

i asked him to cut the splinter out, which generated a concern on his part that i was asking him to cut open my dog even though he didn't know what was in there.

that is a very healthy response from the doctor, but i'd witnessed it happening and knew it was a wood splinter, so i very much appreciated his trust in me as the owner to do the surgery.

and he removed the sticker, and makita is all better now !

the concern on the doctor's part, as well as his flexibility on saving on testing to check for a tumor reflect great service in terms of trying to please a pet owner.

thank you for the great service, jeff<//review>

<pics>None< /pics>< text>
I'm only giving one star, because I have to, but if I had a choice, I would give none.

I brought my 4 month old teacup puppy in after he was showing signs of being wobbly, tired and completely out of it. The doctor, a heavy set Indian man (he never told us his name) came in with zero emotion and did an "exam" on our puppy. His exam consisted of checking his heart beat, his gums and pressing in certain areas of his body; no temperature check and no ear check, which is a pretty common practice when performing a physical exam on any animal.

He then suggested $600 worth of blood tests, x-rays and medications. However, we can't afford that so we opted out of the blood tests and x-rays and just got the medications. He told us our pup would receive a shot to help rehydrate his body and another that would be an antibiotic. However, later in the evening when we were looking up the side effects of the medication he was given since he was showing weakness and pain in his sides and back, we found out it wasn't an antibiotic at all. It was instead an antiemetic which is to help stop vomiting (which wasn't a major concern when we brought him in).

While we were waiting for his shots to be done, a man came in saying that he had called CHP about a cat being hit by a car and was told they brought the cat here...He asked about the cat's well being and they said the cat was very aggressive, and would be sent to the SPCA where they would probably not adopt it out and then put it down. The man wanted to adopt the cat to save it from such a fate, and the same doctor who saw us, tried to talk him out of it. I couldn't believe it!

Do NOT take your pet here ever. They don't care about your animals, they care about their checks. All those "Google User" reviews are fake reviews from the company itself trying to praise themselves so that suckers like us come in. They are absolutely insincere, lack compassion, and really only want as much money as they can get from you...and my dog isn't even better.</text>

It was the first day of their tire sale so they recommended not waiting long to get them if I didn't want to wait for them to be ordered.

That's what I did! Great job on the installation & balancing the next day. They were busy but were able to finish in half the time

First of all, they give you a free tie for an in store review ...   So consider that when reading these 5 star reviews.
1.  Bought a suit there a few weeks ago for an important event this Saturday.   Even though sign outside says $129/for suit, when I checked out they wouldn't honor the sign, but I liked the suit so I paid the $200 extra also paid for alterations at that time.  Extra $30+
2.  The lady working did not take my measurements, instead I tried on different suits of different styles and color in store until I was comfortable.  That should have been my first sign this place was less than a professional suit store.
3.  No one called when my suit came in, I had to keep calling.
4.  Finally someone found my suit, on one of the days I called so I went in to pick it up and have the alterations done.
5.  Jacket was too small.  Workers response..."Its the same size as the suit you tried on that you said fit..."  I said but this one clearly is too small as my sleeves came up to my elbows in front of her.  Her response..."No refunds."
6.  Pants were too big.  Her response, "They came with the jacket."  No refunds, exchange is $50 and will take a week."
7.  No refunds per employee, exchange was going to be $40-50 for each item and take a week.  I had 2 days until my event.
8.  "Alterations only included my pant legs, to hem the waist was another $40-$50 and would take a week".
9.  She would not refund my alterations cost so I could have them done at a real alterations facility, so I let her.   I'm going to try to upload the pant leg Pics that she did from her sewing machine.   It was so bad I had to pay to have it redone at Yoons alterations in Coronado, along with the bringing in the pant waist (total from her $20 by the way).

I'm a business owner, and when my customers are unhappy, I do what I can to make it right.   They refused to correct their wrong measurements, and crappy alterations without charging more money.   Thats why this place is getting a 1 star review.
1.  Wrongly sized cheap suits for high prices with poor customer service...
but hey, at least I got a free tie for writing this Yelp review< /Review>

< review>
My 2nd time here. Their beef "burrito" is their best dish IMO. The beef is cut thin but full of flavor; the wrap is crispy on the outside and chewy on the inside; combined with the bean paste, cucumber, and cilantro it really is a wonder dish to behold.
Dry pot beef is very good as well. Beef is extremely tender. But because it is on par with similar dishes offer by other restaurant, it didn't wow me like their beef burrito did.
My first time there, we also ordered their signature eggplant dish. It was very oily, but very yummy. It's hard to imagine that they could turn a simple eggplant into a entire dish.
After eating there twice, I think that I may return for some beef burrito take out from time to time. And once in a while, I may come for a sit down meal.</review>
